00060   class QCPOptions : public InstanceOptions {
00061   protected:
00063     Driver::DoubleOption _tbf;
00064   public:
00066     QCPOptions(const char* s)
00067     : InstanceOptions(s),
00068       _tbf("tbf", "tie-breaking factor",0.0) {
00069       // Add options
00070       add(_tbf);
00071     }
00073     double tbf(void) const {
00074       return _tbf.value();
00075     }
00077     void tbf(double d) {
00078       _tbf.value(d);
00079     }
00080   };

00084   extern const int* qcp[];
00086   extern const char* name[];
00087 
00089   class Spec {
00090   protected:
00092     const int* data;
00094     int info(int i, int j) const {
00095       int n = data[0];
00096       assert((i >= 0) && (i < n));
00097       assert((j >= 0) && (j < n));
00098       return data[1 + (i * n) + j];
00099     }
00101     static const int* find(const char* s) {
00102       for (int i=0; name[i] != NULL; i++)
00103         if (!strcmp(s,name[i]))
00104           return qcp[i];
00105       return NULL;
00106     }
00107   public:
00109     bool valid(void) const {
00110       return data != NULL;
00111     }
00113     Spec(const char* s) : data(find(s)) {}
00115     int size(void) const {
00116       return data[0];
00117     }
00119     bool assigned(int i, int j) const {
00120       return info(i,j) > 0;
00121     }
00123     int val(int i, int j) const {
00124       assert(assigned(i,j));
00125       return info(i,j) - 1;
00126     }
00127   };
00128 
00129 }
00130 
00131 
00138 class QCP : public Script {
00139 protected:
00141   const QCPOptions& opt;
00143   const Spec spec;
00145   IntVarArray e;
00147   double tbf;
00148 public:
00150   enum {
00151     PROP_BINARY,  
00152     PROP_DISTINCT 
00153   };
00155   enum {
00156     BRANCH_SIZE,     
00157     BRANCH_AFC_SIZE, 
00158   };
00160   QCP(const QCPOptions& opt0)
00161     : Script(opt0),
00162       opt(opt0), spec(opt.instance()),
00163       e(*this, spec.size() * spec.size(), 0, spec.size()-1) {
00164     // Problem size
00165     int n = spec.size();
00166     // Matrix for elements
00167     Matrix<IntVarArray> m(e, n);
00168 
00169     // Assign fields
00170     for (int i=0; i<n; i++)
00171       for (int j=0; j<n; j++)
00172         if (spec.assigned(i,j))
00173           rel(*this, m(i,j) == spec.val(i,j));
00174 
00175     // Post constraints
00176     switch (opt.propagation()) {
00177     case PROP_BINARY:
00178       for (int i=0; i<n; i++)
00179         for (int k=0; k<n; k++)
00180           for (int l=k+1; l<n; l++) {
00181             rel(*this, m(i,k) != m(i,l));
00182             rel(*this, m(k,i) != m(l,i));
00183           }
00184       break;
00185     case PROP_DISTINCT:
00186       for (int i=0; i<n; i++) {
00187         distinct(*this, m.row(i), opt.ipl());
00188         distinct(*this, m.col(i), opt.ipl());
00189       }
00190       break;
00191     }
00192 
00193     if (opt.assets() == 0) {
00194       // Post branchers directly, as no portfolio search requested
00195       switch (opt.branching()) {
00196       case BRANCH_SIZE:
00197         branch(*this, e, INT_VAR_SIZE_MIN(), INT_VAL_MIN());
00198         break;
00199       case BRANCH_AFC_SIZE:
00200         branch(*this, e, INT_VAR_AFC_SIZE_MAX(opt.decay()), INT_VAL_MIN());
00201         break;
00202       }
00203     }
00204   }
00206   virtual bool slave(const MetaInfo& mi) {
00207     if (mi.type() == MetaInfo::PORTFOLIO) {
00208       double tbf = opt.tbf();
00209       Rnd r(seeds[mi.asset() % n_seeds]);
00210       switch (opt.branching()) {
00211       case BRANCH_SIZE:
00212         {
00213           auto tbl =
00214             [tbf] (const Space&, double w, double b) {
00215               assert(w >= b);
00216               return b + (w - b) * tbf;
00217             };
00218           branch(*this, e, tiebreak(INT_VAR_SIZE_MIN(tbl),
00219                                     INT_VAR_RND(r)),
00220                  INT_VAL_MIN());
00221         }
00222         break;
00223       case BRANCH_AFC_SIZE:
00224         {
00225           auto tbl =
00226             [tbf] (const Space&, double w, double b) {
00227               assert(b >= w);
00228               return b - (b - w) * tbf;
00229             };
00230           branch(*this, e, tiebreak(INT_VAR_AFC_SIZE_MAX(opt.decay(), tbl),
00231                                     INT_VAR_RND(r)),
00232                  INT_VAL_MIN());
00233         }
00234         break;
00235       default: ;
00236       }
00237     }
00238     return true;
00239   }
00241   QCP(QCP& s)
00242     : Script(s), opt(s.opt), spec(s.spec) {
00243     e.update(*this, s.e);
00244   }
00246   virtual Space*
00247   copy(void) {
00248     return new QCP(*this);
00249   }
00251   virtual void
00252   print(std::ostream& os) const {
00253     int n = spec.size();
00254     Matrix<IntVarArray> m(e, n);
00255 
00256     for (int i=0; i<n; i++) {
00257       os << "\t";
00258       for (int j=0; j<n; j++) {
00259         if (m(i,j).assigned())
00260           os.width(2);
00261         os << m(i,j) << " ";
00262       }
00263       os << std::endl;
00264     }
00265   }
00266 };
00267 
00271 int
00272 main(int argc, char* argv[]) {
00273  QCPOptions opt("QCP");
00274 
00275   opt.branching(QCP::BRANCH_AFC_SIZE);
00276   opt.branching(QCP::BRANCH_SIZE, "size");
00277   opt.branching(QCP::BRANCH_AFC_SIZE, "afc");
00278 
00279   opt.propagation(QCP::PROP_DISTINCT);
00280   opt.propagation(QCP::PROP_BINARY, "binary",
00281                       "only binary disequality constraints");
00282   opt.propagation(QCP::PROP_DISTINCT, "distinct",
00283                       "distinct constraints");
00284 
00285   opt.instance(name[0]);
00286 
00287   opt.parse(argc,argv);
00288   if (!Spec(opt.instance()).valid()) {
00289     std::cerr << "Error: unkown instance" << std::endl;
00290     return 1;
00291   }
00292   Script::run<QCP,DFS,QCPOptions>(opt);
00293   return 0;
00294 }
